This store is a gem that should be supported. They are holding down space for black-owned business in Oakland with high intentions of community service, quality art from local artists, important literature, insence, jewelry and wellness/beauty products made from family recipes. All the beautiful brothers and sisters involved in this business are amazing to talk to. It's worth dropping by just to get to know them.

And it's also worth dropping into their Soul Food spot two doors down where they offer delicious and healthy vegan and halal meat options.

These are the types of business and families the community should support!</Review>
